\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00383}00383       \textcolor{comment}{// loop over the velocities. Calculate each section separately instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00384}00384 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00385}00385       \textcolor{comment}{// Norm calculation involves the double contraction of two tensors, so we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00386}00386       \textcolor{comment}{// take the summation of nine separate components for clarity. Fortunately}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00387}00387       \textcolor{comment}{// most of the components zero out in the axisymmetric case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00388}00388       \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00389}00389       \textcolor{comment}{// Entry (1,1) in dyad matrix}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00391}00391       \textcolor{comment}{// Entry (1,2) in dyad matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00392}00392       \textcolor{comment}{// No contribution}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01744}01744           \textcolor{comment}{// Subtract the mesh velocity terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01745}01745           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1SphericalNavierStokesEquations_ae99a23d65958a96ae2d90151b86d30ab}{ALE\_is\_disabled}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01746}01746           \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01747}01747             sum -\/= scaled\_re\_st *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01748}01748                    (mesh\_velocity[0] * interpolated\_dudx(0, 0) * r +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01749}01749                     mesh\_velocity[1] * (interpolated\_dudx(0, 1) -\/ u\_theta)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01750}01750                    r * sin\_theta * testf[l];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01751}01751           \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01752}01752 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01753}01753           \textcolor{comment}{// Add the Coriolis term}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01754}01754           sum -\/= 2.0 * scaled\_re\_inv\_ro * sin\_theta * u\_phi * r2 * sin\_theta *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01755}01755                  testf[l];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01756}01756 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01757}01757           \textcolor{comment}{// r-\/derivative test function component of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01758}01758           sum += (-\/interpolated\_p + 2.0 * interpolated\_dudx(0, 0)) * r2 *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01759}01759                  sin\_theta * dtestfdx(l, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01760}01760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01761}01761           \textcolor{comment}{// theta-\/derivative test function component of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01762}01762           sum +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01763}01763             (r * interpolated\_dudx(1, 0) -\/ u\_theta + interpolated\_dudx(0, 1)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01764}01764             sin\_theta * dtestfdx(l, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01765}01765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01766}01766           \textcolor{comment}{// Undifferentiated test function component of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01767}01767           sum += 2.0 *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01768}01768                  ((-\/r * interpolated\_p + interpolated\_dudx(1, 1) + 2.0 * u\_r) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01769}01769                     sin\_theta +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01770}01770                   u\_theta * cos\_theta) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01771}01771                  testf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01772}01772 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01773}01773           \textcolor{comment}{// Make the residuals negative for consistency with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01774}01774           \textcolor{comment}{// other Navier-\/Stokes equations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01775}01775           residuals[local\_eqn] -\/= sum * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01779}01779           \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01780}01780             \textcolor{comment}{// Loop over the velocity shape functions again}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01901}01901             \textcolor{comment}{// Now loop over pressure shape functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01902}01902             \textcolor{comment}{// This is the contribution from pressure gradient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01903}01903             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} l2 = 0; l2 < n\_pres; l2++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01904}01904             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01905}01905               \textcolor{comment}{/*If we are at a non-\/zero degree of freedom in the entry*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01906}01906               local\_unknown = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1SphericalNavierStokesEquations_ad8d9a0edbe3793a008a6bff670c26643}{p\_local\_eqn}}(l2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01907}01907               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_unknown >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01908}01908               \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01909}01909                 jacobian(local\_eqn, local\_unknown) +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01910}01910                   psip(l2) * (r2 * dtestfdx(l, 0) + 2.0 * r * testf(l)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01911}01911                   sin\_theta * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01912}01912               \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01913}01913             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01914}01914           \} \textcolor{comment}{// End of Jacobian calculation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01915}01915 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01916}01916         \} \textcolor{comment}{// End of if not boundary condition statement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01917}01917           \textcolor{comment}{// End of r-\/component momentum equation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01918}01918 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01919}01919 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01920}01920         \textcolor{comment}{// SECOND: theta-\/component momentum equation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01921}01921 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01922}01922         \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_adb50e893b86b3e55e751a42eab3cba82}{i}} = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01923}01923 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01924}01924         \textcolor{comment}{// IF it's not a boundary condition}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01925}01925         local\_eqn = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1FiniteElement_a5da80bbed97543e586f698251d67941d}{nodal\_local\_eqn}}(l, u\_nodal\_index[\mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_adb50e893b86b3e55e751a42eab3cba82}{i}}]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01926}01926         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_eqn >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01927}01927         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01928}01928           \textcolor{comment}{// All convective terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01929}01929           \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} conv = (u\_r * interpolated\_dudx(1, 0) * r +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01930}01930                          u\_theta * interpolated\_dudx(1, 1) + u\_r * u\_theta) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01931}01931                           sin\_theta -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01932}01932                         u\_phi * u\_phi * cos\_theta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01933}01933 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01934}01934           \textcolor{comment}{// Add the time-\/derivative and convective terms to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01935}01935           \textcolor{comment}{// residuals sum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01936}01936           \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} sum =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01937}01937             (scaled\_re\_st * dudt[1] * r2 * sin\_theta + scaled\_re * r * conv) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01938}01938             testf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01939}01939 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01940}01940           \textcolor{comment}{// Subtract the mesh velocity terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01941}01941           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1SphericalNavierStokesEquations_ae99a23d65958a96ae2d90151b86d30ab}{ALE\_is\_disabled}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01942}01942           \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01943}01943             sum -\/= scaled\_re\_st *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01944}01944                    (mesh\_velocity[0] * interpolated\_dudx(1, 0) * r +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01945}01945                     mesh\_velocity[1] * (interpolated\_dudx(1, 1) + u\_r)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01946}01946                    r * sin\_theta * testf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01947}01947           \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01948}01948 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01949}01949           \textcolor{comment}{// Add the Coriolis term}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01950}01950           sum -\/= 2.0 * scaled\_re\_inv\_ro * cos\_theta * u\_phi * r2 * sin\_theta *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01951}01951                  testf[l];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01952}01952 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01953}01953           \textcolor{comment}{// r-\/derivative test function component of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01954}01954           sum +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01955}01955             (r * interpolated\_dudx(1, 0) -\/ u\_theta + interpolated\_dudx(0, 1)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01956}01956             r * sin\_theta * dtestfdx(l, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01957}01957 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01958}01958           \textcolor{comment}{// theta-\/derivative test function component of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01959}01959           sum +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01960}01960             (-\/r * interpolated\_p + 2.0 * interpolated\_dudx(1, 1) + 2.0 * u\_r) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01961}01961             dtestfdx(l, 1) * sin\_theta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01962}01962 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01963}01963           \textcolor{comment}{// Undifferentiated test function component of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01964}01964           sum -\/=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01965}01965             ((r * interpolated\_dudx(1, 0) -\/ u\_theta + interpolated\_dudx(0, 1)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01966}01966                sin\_theta -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01967}01967              (-\/r * interpolated\_p + 2.0 * u\_r + 2.0 * u\_theta * cot\_theta) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01968}01968                cos\_theta) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01969}01969             testf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01970}01970 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01971}01971           \textcolor{comment}{// Add the sum to the residuals,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01972}01972           \textcolor{comment}{//(Negative for consistency)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01973}01973           residuals[local\_eqn] -\/= sum * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01974}01974 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01975}01975           \textcolor{comment}{// CALCULATE THE JACOBIAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01976}01976           \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (flag)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01977}01977           \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01978}01978             \textcolor{comment}{// Loop over the velocity shape functions again}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01979}01979             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} l2 = 0; l2 < n\_node; l2++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01980}01980             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01981}01981               \textcolor{comment}{// Cannot loop over the velocity components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01982}01982               \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/-\/ need to compute these separately instead}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01988}01988               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_unknown >= 0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01990}01990                 \textcolor{comment}{// No time derivative contribution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01991}01991 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01992}01992                 \textcolor{comment}{// Convective terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01993}01993                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} jac\_sum = scaled\_re *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01994}01994                                  (r2 * interpolated\_dudx(1, 0) + r * u\_theta) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01995}01995                                  psif(l2) * sin\_theta * testf(l);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l01998}01998                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1SphericalNavierStokesEquations_ae99a23d65958a96ae2d90151b86d30ab}{ALE\_is\_disabled}})}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02000}02000                   jac\_sum -\/= scaled\_re\_st * mesh\_velocity[1] * psif(l2) * r *}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02002}02002                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02003}02003 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02004}02004                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the r-\/derivative}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02008}02008                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the theta-\/derivative test function}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02017}02017 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02019}02019                 jacobian(local\_eqn, local\_unknown) -\/= jac\_sum * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02020}02020               \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02021}02021               \textcolor{comment}{// End of i2=0 section}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02022}02022 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02023}02023 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02024}02024               i2 = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02025}02025 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02026}02026               \textcolor{comment}{// If at a non-\/zero degree of freedom add in the entry}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02027}02027               local\_unknown = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1FiniteElement_a5da80bbed97543e586f698251d67941d}{nodal\_local\_eqn}}(l2, u\_nodal\_index[i2]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02028}02028               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_unknown >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02029}02029               \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02030}02030                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the convective terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02031}02031                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} jac\_conv = r * u\_r * dpsifdx(l2, 0) +}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02033}02033                                   (interpolated\_dudx(1, 1) + u\_r) * psif(l2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02034}02034 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02035}02035                 \textcolor{comment}{// Add the time-\/derivative term and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02036}02036                 \textcolor{comment}{// convective terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02037}02037                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} jac\_sum =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02038}02038                   (scaled\_re\_st * \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1FiniteElement_a9addfe893ab8205619963aa96204cdc4}{node\_pt}}(l2)-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1Data_a065d7bffcec82bf4d4bd7b41f9aa80b3}{time\_stepper\_pt}}()-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TimeStepper_a4cb0aecb044b77ba0553cdd54b586d8a}{weight}}(1, 0) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02039}02039                      psif(l2) * r2 +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02040}02040                    scaled\_re * r * jac\_conv) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02041}02041                   testf(l) * sin\_theta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02042}02042 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02043}02043 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02044}02044                 \textcolor{comment}{// Mesh velocity terms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02045}02045                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1SphericalNavierStokesEquations_ae99a23d65958a96ae2d90151b86d30ab}{ALE\_is\_disabled}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02046}02046                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02047}02047                   jac\_sum -\/= scaled\_re\_st *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02048}02048                              (mesh\_velocity[0] * dpsifdx(l2, 0) * r +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02049}02049                               mesh\_velocity[1] * dpsifdx(l2, 1)) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02050}02050                              r * sin\_theta * testf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02051}02051                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02052}02052 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02053}02053                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the r-\/derivative test function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02054}02054                 \textcolor{comment}{// part of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02055}02055                 jac\_sum += (r * dpsifdx(l2, 0) -\/ psif(l2)) * r *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02056}02056                            dtestfdx(l, 0) * sin\_theta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02057}02057 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02058}02058                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the theta-\/derivative test function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02059}02059                 \textcolor{comment}{// part of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02060}02060                 jac\_sum += 2.0 * dpsifdx(l2, 1) * dtestfdx(l, 1) * sin\_theta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02061}02061 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02062}02062                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the undifferentiated test function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02063}02063                 \textcolor{comment}{// part of stress tensor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02064}02064                 jac\_sum -\/= ((r * dpsifdx(l2, 0) -\/ psif(l2)) * sin\_theta -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02065}02065                             2.0 * psif(l2) * cot\_theta * cos\_theta) *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02066}02066                            testf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02067}02067 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02068}02068                 \textcolor{comment}{// Add the contribution to the jacobian}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02069}02069                 jacobian(local\_eqn, local\_unknown) -\/= jac\_sum * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02070}02070 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02071}02071                 \textcolor{comment}{// Mass matrix term}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02072}02072                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (flag == 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02073}02073                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02074}02074                   mass\_matrix(local\_eqn, local\_unknown) +=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02075}02075                     scaled\_re\_st * psif[l2] * testf[l] * r2 * sin\_theta * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02076}02076                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02077}02077               \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02078}02078               \textcolor{comment}{// End of i2=1 section}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02080}02080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02081}02081               i2 = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02082}02082 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02083}02083               \textcolor{comment}{// If at a non-\/zero degree of freedom add in the entry}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02084}02084               local\_unknown = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1FiniteElement_a5da80bbed97543e586f698251d67941d}{nodal\_local\_eqn}}(l2, u\_nodal\_index[i2]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02085}02085               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_unknown >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02086}02086               \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02087}02087                 \textcolor{comment}{// Only a convective term contribution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02088}02088                 jacobian(local\_eqn, local\_unknown) += scaled\_re * 2.0 * r *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02089}02089                                                       psif(l2) * u\_phi *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02090}02090                                                       cos\_theta * testf(l) * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02091}02091 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02094}02094                   2.0 * scaled\_re\_inv\_ro * cos\_theta * psif(l2) * r2 *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02095}02095                   sin\_theta * testf[l] * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02096}02096               \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02097}02097               \textcolor{comment}{// End of i2=2 section}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02098}02098             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02099}02099             \textcolor{comment}{// End of the l2 loop over the test functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02100}02100 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02101}02101             \textcolor{comment}{/*Now loop over pressure shape functions*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02102}02102             \textcolor{comment}{/*This is the contribution from pressure gradient*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02103}02103             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} l2 = 0; l2 < n\_pres; l2++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02104}02104             \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02106}02106               local\_unknown = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1SphericalNavierStokesEquations_ad8d9a0edbe3793a008a6bff670c26643}{p\_local\_eqn}}(l2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02107}02107               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_unknown >= 0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02129}02129           \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} conv = u\_r * interpolated\_dudx(2, 0) * r * sin\_theta;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02134}02134           \textcolor{comment}{// Remaining convective terms}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02136}02136 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02137}02137           \textcolor{comment}{// Add the time-\/derivative term and the convective terms to the sum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02138}02138           \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} sum =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02139}02139             (scaled\_re\_st * r2 * dudt[2] * sin\_theta + scaled\_re * conv * r) *}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02146}02146                    (mesh\_velocity[0] * interpolated\_dudx(2, 0) * r +}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02214}02214                 jacobian(local\_eqn, local\_unknown) -\/=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02215}02215                   2.0 * scaled\_re\_inv\_ro * cos\_theta * psif(l2) * r2 *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02216}02216                   sin\_theta * testf[l] * \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_1_1QuadTreeNames_a8954a5947b19986b8c4b755bc7639f7daabab2a070c062503375f8264f1b6d7d6}{W}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02217}02217               \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02218}02218               \textcolor{comment}{// End of i2=1 section}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02219}02219 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02220}02220 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02221}02221               i2 = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02222}02222 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02223}02223               \textcolor{comment}{// If at a non-\/zero degree of freedom add in the entry}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02224}02224               local\_unknown = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1FiniteElement_a5da80bbed97543e586f698251d67941d}{nodal\_local\_eqn}}(l2, u\_nodal\_index[i2]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02225}02225               \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (local\_unknown >= 0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02228}02228                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} jac\_conv = r * u\_r * dpsifdx(l2, 0) * sin\_theta;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02233}02233                 \textcolor{comment}{// Contribution from the remaining convective terms}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{spherical__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l02236}02236                 \textcolor{comment}{// Add the convective and time derivatives}}
